Beautiful campground! The staff is very friendly and they go above and beyond to make your stay the best way possible. They even opened the pool up for our daughter's! Sites are plenty big for our 40ft 5th wheel. Campground is orderly and kept clean. The views are amazing and at night it gets very quiet to the point you can hear the cows from the distance. It's right off the highway but the road noise is to a minimum. They even have trails to explore and the pet area is nicely maintained. The nearest WalMart is 27mins away and Ace Hardware etc. Carsen city is 40mins away if your looking for more options like Home Depot, In and Out. burger, Target etc.< /Text>

<Text>Friendly team, "million dollar views" and impeccably clean.<//Text>< Rate>

<Gmap_id>0x80977eae89810ec1:0xe60d558583609059< /Gmap_id>< UserId.>
101102286195924985942</UserId.>
< Time>
1598580866012</Time>
<Pictures>None< /Pictures></record></dataset><record>
<rating>5<//rating><Resp>None< /Resp>< Review>
The family and I love this place and are here often. The bathrooms, laundry room, pool, playground, game room, and other amenities are very clean and well maintained. We have stayed in the camp ground in our trailer and in a couple of different rooms in the hotel. We have always had a pleasant experience. The new owners are constantly making updates and improvements. We had good experiences with the previous owners and the new owners have also been great to work with. If you are visiting in the summer, Walker Burger and Mountain View BBQ are great places to eat and are about five minutes down the road in Walker. The restaurants are seasonal though, so they may be closed if you visit close to winter. Fly fishing in the Walker river is great and there are public waters about ten minutes up the road. Walker Coffee Company recently opened in Walker and the owner, Scott, is a fishing and hunting guide for the area. Walker Coffee also sells some flies and tackle. There are also countless 4X4 trails nearby and the Eastern Sierra ATV Jamboree is held in this area every year in September. Make sure you book in advance if you want to come in September as all the local hotels and campgrounds are usually booked up. The wifi here was recently upgraded and is pretty fast. I believe you can also pay additional to get access to an even faster wifi if you want. I've heard AT&T doesn't have great cell service here, but I have Verizon and get decent service. We have a signal booster in our trailer and that boosts it to full bars for us. We are active duty military and the owners, and this area in general, are very friendly and supportive to military.< /Review>

<Text>Wow! What a great place. We stayed here from Friday to Monday on Memorial Day weekend 2019. Great hospitality, very level RV sites, super clean restrooms and showers. We took Topaz ave back to the 395 and let me tell you, the scenery is absolutely amazing. Beautiful picturesque, snowy mountains, grazing cattle, and a view of the entire valley. <userid>107615490205093230448< /userid>< Text>
Fun bar...Nothing fancy.  A basic bar and a good place for a few drinks.  The special was a free Sol beer with purchase of a shot of tequila.  One customer asked for a fancy multi-ingredient cocktail and the bartender (I believe his name was Parker) responded, "We serve drinks with up to 3 ingredients...ice is one of them."  Go if you like a fun no-nonsense bar and a some funny, sassy sarcasm from the bartender. If you're fussy, needy and thin-skinned don't go, you'll hate it.</Text>

<Rate>1</Rate>< text>
The carved sign says cocktails. The ambiance screams local dive bar. Both great indicators of at the very least, an interesting experience. It doesn't have to be a fantastic drink but work with what you have. Our initial experience was a walk by on our way to dinner, the bartender was pleasant and let us know that they serve simple drinks and are open late (2am). When we returned, a different bartender did nothing but insult my wife and I and eventually refused to serve us even though we were simply asking what we did to offend him.

If you're looking for a place that is trying to stay relevant and to be the "blue collar" Carmel, then this is the place for you. Totally unoriginal rip off of an episode of Shameless, this place will do nothing to enhance your experience of Carmel.

This place might be for you if you're looking to have unsolicited insults hurled your way if you don't dress, act, speak, or look middle class white generic, appearing in a way that makes the bartenders subjectively feel better about their rock bottom place in life.

The unfortunate part is that this place thrives off bad reviews and even encourages them. Catering to the two local, middle aged people at the bar, the Carny bartender mentioned three times that we were millennials and should leave Yelp reviews.

Save yourself time and hassle and just walk by knowing that you are better than the scum bag, local patrons and trolls that are employed there.

As a result of this place we will not return to this tourist trap city. Everything is over priced, over promised and takes itself way too seriously.< /text>

< Text>
Let me tell you! Since Sorrento's first owners, I thought this place was never going to be the same. The second owners, despite their efforts ran Sorrento's into the ground! After hearing that they would be closing (no surprise, it was all a matter of time) I got really disappointed... I thought "Maaan! what is it going to be now? ANOTHER Asian restaurant?!" Well to my delightful surprise, Calabria Brothers bought it out and kept it as an Italian deli!

When I first walked in, I was taken aback a bit. I was used to the cluttered aisles full of Italian goods, but no longer. It was incredibly spacious! Even with tables and chairs to actually sit down and eat! It looked wonderful, they didn't sacrifice anything fully utilizing the floorspace there! Clean, spacious and very welcoming.

The one guy who prepares the sandwiches, I always forget to catch his name, is really friendly and makes the sandwiches flawlessly in my opinion.

The sandwiches are portioned VERY well, I have to say AND very reasonably priced! Opposed to the second regime of Sorrento's owners who began making their sandwiches much smaller and more expensive!

This really took me back to the old school Sorrento's. But, since it's been that long since I've had a decent Italian cut sandwich, I have to say that Calabria Brothers sandwiches are BETTER!

They have outstanding choices of meats and cheeses, even bread! Adding in Ciabatta and Wheat bread. The sandwiches all come with your choice of having mustard, mayo, salt, pepper, olive oil, home made vinegar, and their garlic/pesto spread. Honestly some amazing sandwiches!

I also can't forget, you can also get all your quality cold cuts and cheeses there too. They also do catering.

In sum, MOST awesome Italian deli around! You have to come and try it, and unless you're not a fan of big Italian deli sandwiches, you're going to love it!

Mangiare e godere!

*Review by J.Pedroza from 2012 around the time of it's grand opening.<//Text>

< text>
Management and employees are top tier here.
I went in to purchase a set of furniture, the employee/greeter was quick to help me carry it and we noticed that it had slight damage, he quickly called over a manager who also reviewed the pieces. Manger then took the time to explain why/how it likely happened, as well as how I could fix it if I choose to. He then offered me a very 'generous' mark down due to the damages, all without me ever having to bicker or complain, they simply helped me out and ensured that I was satisfied. (This was on 7/7/20 6ish)
Employee/doorman then helped me load up the furniture and we were on our way.
Me and my girl friend are moving into our first place together and this was an extremely relieving and exciting experience as this was our first furniture purchase in what was a very lengthy and stressful process of moving.

I'm extremely grateful for their assistance and level of customer care, I will go out of my way to return to the store specifically and will spread the word to family and friends as well.
In addition this store actually does have a very good selection and is a little larger/laid out in a way that I prefer.</text>

< Review>
As you know
Tuesday starts at $6.00
Wednesday $4.00
Thursday $2.00
Friday 1.00
Saturday 0.25
Sometimes in the early morning when the store opens there is a very long line of people waiting to enter. There are shopping carts to use while shopping. Once inside the store, you will see large wooden boxes, they are filled with items. Some items may not be worth what you can purchase them in a regular store. Some items my be less than what they would cost in a regular store. Some of the food items have expired dates on them and some don't. There are household items,toys, food,clothes, office supplies and much more. Every day the merchandise changes, you never know what will be for sale. Thursday I bought 4 decks of Bicycle playing cards for $2.00. Think of it as a treasure hunt, be careful when buying items here stop and think what would it cost in a regular store.< /Review>
